------------------------------------
Student Status - Microsoft Community

wayneweiss say:

Student Status

Hi Everyone,

Can I change the graduation date of my student status because I have to take a leave of absence?

jiaxing bian msft say:

Hi Wayne,

In Office 365, we control students’ access to their education account by assigning or removing the license, instead of the graduation date.

If you’re taking a leave, please contact your administrator, and he will determine whether it’s necessary to remove your license.

Note: If your license is removed, you will lose access to the online services and data, including:

1. All data that is associated with that student account is held for 30 days with the exception of data held with Legal Hold which is kept for the duration of the hold

2. After the 30-day grace period, the data is deleted and can’t be recovered, except for documents that are saved in SharePoint Online sites

For more detailed information, refer to this article below:

Manage graduating student licenses and content in Office 365 Education

Regards,
Jiaxing

learning_tools,

Nokia 1680 connectivity with PC through serial cable - Microsoft Community

shehzad786 say:

Nokia 1680 connectivity with PC through serial cable

shahzad hanif

psychomania---01 say: That model does not support an official nokia cable connection to a PC for transferring files.

What you have is an unofficial product that may cause damage to your phone.

You need to contact the store/person that sold it to you for support. We cannot help you here with unofficial products.

intexture say:

I have Data Cable for Nokia 1680 and i am perfectly able to transfer data.

 

All you need is to install the data cable on some COM, on my PC it was installed on COM8

Then in Nokia PC suite, Go to Manage Connections in Settings and in the Data Cable option, check appropirate COM Port.

 

And phone gets connected, we can transfer anything between phone and PC.

 

If you want help for anything in more detail PM me.

 

 

Regards

Salman

 

Moderators note.

Personal Info removed.

 

Message Edited by shameers on 09-Feb-2009 10:11 AM

grschinon say: It may be technically possible to transfer files between your computer and a 1680 this way, but it doesn't alter the fact that this is software that is not sanctioned by Nokia. Its use may damage your phone, in which case your warranty will be invalidated.

grschinon say: You bought a low-end 1xxx series phone that has a camera for taking pictures intended for sending by MMS. If you want officially supported connectivity of any kind with your computer you need to use a 2xxx series phone at least.

While cable connectivity may be technically possible with a 1680 it involves the use of hardware and software not supported, supplied or even authorized by Nokia. Use it at your own risk. If they do damage your phone you're on your own.

Power point 2013 - can't print - Microsoft Community

svetlapotter say:

Power point 2013 - can't print

I am trying to print a ppt presentation, but the printer just starts as if it will print but nothing comes out.  There are no documents shown in the printer queue.

It is not the printer as it prints ppt fine from other computers on the network.  From my pc, no ppt can be printed. Other word or excel documents print fine.

I saved the ppt doc as pdf and then it prints fine.  This is a new issue as I was able to print ppt before, but have not used the program for some time.

Have restarted the pc a number of times...

Any thoughts?

vijay a. verma say:
Please try these options one by one and check after each option.

1. Sometimes, add-ins can cause problems. To determine, if add-in is a problem start your application in safe mode and see if problem has gone away.

To start in Safe Mode -

Hold CTRL key and click on application icon and don't release the CTRL key till it asks you for Safe mode confirmation.

If yes, then start application normally and disable add-ins one by one and start application again every time you disable an add-in to determine the culprit add-in.
To disable add-in > File > Options > Add-ins > Down below you have Manage: Com Add-in : Press Go > Untick the Add-ins to disable and tick to enable them

2. Try repairing your Office installation. First try Quick Repair (takes 5 - 10 mins) , if that doesn't help then try Online Repair (Takes more than 30 mins but less than 1 hour in general)

Note for Office 2013 and below - Please repair only if you have product key with you as sometimes it asks for the product key again after the repair.

Windows Key+I > Apps > Locate Office & click > Modify > Quick repair / Online repair

svetlapotter say:

HI

Safe  mode allowed me to print.  I checked the addins - I only have two addins - one of which was ticked (OneNote Linked Notes ), so I unticked in, restarted ppt - no success.

What do you think I should try next?

Thanks for your help.

vijay a. verma say:
Move to repair. Also, try to reinstall the driver of printer again before repair.

svetlapotter say: just to check a detail - the addins - should they be inactive or disabled?  Mine are inactive not disabled.  Does it make any difference?

vijay a. verma say:
They should be inactive.

Counting Duplicates (Round 2) - Microsoft Community

zm 1 say:

Counting Duplicates (Round 2)

In another thread, I had asked about a way to count duplicate addresses in an Excel-based address list so that I can "household" the data by consolidating the many people of a house into just a single house.  The trick rested in the use of a COUNTIFS formula, like the one below (see the other post here).  But this time around, I am not getting the outputs I would expect.  I'm not able to identify what may be a problem...

In this file, addresses are organized quite rigorously in the following way:
Column F: House Number
Column G: House Fraction
Column H: Street Pre-Direction
Column I: Street Name
Column J: Street Suffix
Column K: Street Post-Direction
Column L: Building Number
Column M: Apartment Number
Column N: City
Column O: State
Column P: Zip Code

I used this formula in Column Q, eliminating state and zip code from the equation...
=COUNTIFS(F$2:F2,F2,G$2:G2,G2,H$2:H2,H2,I$2:I2,I2,J$2:J2,J2, K$2:K2,K2,L$2:L2,L2,M$2:M2,M2)

What Excel returns to me is a 0 when I should always have a value equal or greater than 1.

What to do??

Thanks!
Zakhary
ashish mathur say:

Hi,

 

Try this

 

in cell Q2, enter this formula and copy down

 

=F2&G2&H2&I2&J2&K2&L2&M2

 

In cell R2, enter =COUNTIF(Q$2:Q2,Q2) and copy down.

 

What result do you now get?

Deactivating Office 2007 from pc - Microsoft Community

graemestantiall say:

Deactivating Office 2007 from pc

Hi. Is it possible to deactivate office 2007 home and student from a computer as it is only allowed to be activated 5 times and after this will now allow use of. I can not find anything on the product itself to do this. Thanks. My hope is that if this is possible I can continue to use it on further purchased pc's

doug robbins - mvp office apps & services (word) say:

I do not know of any suite of Office 2007 that allowed installation on 5 computers (read the EULA for your version by clicking on Help and then About Microsoft Office in one of the applications (e.g. Word) and then click on the View the End-User License Agreement link.


However, if you uninstall the software from one computer and install it on another (for which you will of course need the Product Key) you can activated it by using the phone activation method.


If in response to the prompts, it tells you that you have reached the limit of activations, call again and ignore the prompts until a person comes on the line.

Internet explorer will not load google.com or some other webpages - Microsoft Community

timothya say:

Internet explorer will not load google.com or some other webpages

Internet Explorer 8 will not load google.com and some other webpages. Bing opens and Windows update opens. Google.com just sits and try to load. Other PC on the same network are OK.
halima s say:

Hi timothyA,

 

1.    When was the last time it was working fine?

2.    Do you have any security software installed on the computer?

3.    Do you receive any error message?

Method 1

Check if any add-ons on the Internet explorer are causing the error. I would suggest you to try opening Internet explorer in the no add-ons mode.

a)   Click the  Start button, click  All Programs, and click Accessories

b)   Click  System Tools, and then click  Internet Explorer (No Add-ons).

 

Refer the link below for more information.

http://windows.microsoft.com/en-us/Windows7/How-do-browser-add-ons-affect-my-computer

 

Method 2

This may also happen if the Internet Explorer browser settings are incorrect. I would suggest that you reset the browser settings to default and check if it works.

For more information refer the below link.

How to reset Internet Explorer settings

http://support.microsoft.com/kb/923737

Important:  Reset Internet Explorer to its default configuration. This step will also disable any add-ons, plug-ins, or toolbars that are installed. Although this solution is quick, it also means that, if you want to use any of those add-ons in the future, they must be reinstalled.

 

Hope this helps!

Halima S   - Microsoft Support.

Visit our  Microsoft Answers Feedback Forum and let us know what you think.

    X double Bar Symbol X with two bars above it. HELP - Microsoft Community

    franalb say:

    X double Bar Symbol X with two bars above it. HELP

    How does one create the statistics symbol X double bar, that is an x with two bars above it.  I can see it in the equation editor (Cambria Math font) but can't seem to find in in the insert symbol area under that font.  Using the equation tool puts the symbol into a text box and I'm trying into use it in a cell
    hansv mvp say:

    You can create a "combining double overline", but if you do it outside the Equation Editor, it doesn't work well - the alignment with other characters looks OK in the formula bar, but it is off in the cell itself. If you want to try it:

    Type an x in a cell.

    Activate the Insert tab of the ribbon and click Symbol.

    Make sure that Unicode (hex) is selected in the from dropdown.

    Select (normal text) from the Font dropdown, and Combining Diacritical Marks from the Subset dropdown.

    Scroll down a row or two, and you should see the Combining Double Overline (not to be confused with the similar looking Modifier Letter Unaspirated). Its character code is 033F.

    Select it, then click Insert, and close the Symbol dialog.

    Look at the formula bar and at the cell...
